<script type='text/Javascript'>
       function toggleSection (secid) {
         var secEl = document.getElementById(secid);
         var linkEl = document.getElementById(secid + '-title');
         if (secEl.className == 'section-shown') {
           secEl.className = 'section-hidden';
           linkEl.innerHTML = linkEl.innerHTML.replace('\u25bc', '\u25b6');
         } else {
           secEl.className = 'section-shown';
           linkEl.innerHTML = linkEl.innerHTML.replace('\u25b6', '\u25bc');
         }}
	</script>
<!--end linklist的收放功能-->
